<div id="review_435521679" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/435521679" />
    <a title="Aму" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10342872-a"><img alt="Aму" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411959522p2/10342872.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/435521679?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aму" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aму" href="/user/show/10342872-a">Aму</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780988489134" href="/book/show/16100228-consequences">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10342872-a?shelf=kidnapped-or-forced">kidnapped-or-forced</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer435521679" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4825612510740339413">Anthony Rawlings is the biggest prick that I have ever had the NON-pleasure of coming in contact with. Had my Mother not taught me better, I would be plotting how to rip off his genitals. :)<br/><br/>My review will be featuring (<b>Note</b>: I say FEATURING not ANSWERING.) the four main questions that have been plaguing everyone's mind since/before reading this book. - Let us dive right in.<br/><br/><u>What the fuck did I just read</u><b>?</b><br/><br/>Consequences is all about the cause and effect of people. (So whoever marked the genre as <i>BDSM</i></span>
  <span id="freeText4825612510740339413" style="display:none">Anthony Rawlings is the biggest prick that I have ever had the NON-pleasure of coming in contact with. Had my Mother not taught me better, I would be plotting how to rip off his genitals. :)<br /><br />My review will be featuring (<b>Note</b>: I say FEATURING not ANSWERING.) the four main questions that have been plaguing everyone's mind since/before reading this book. - Let us dive right in.<br /><br /><u>What the fuck did I just read</u><b>?</b><br /><br />Consequences is all about the cause and effect of people. (So whoever marked the genre as <i>BDSM</i> and <i>Erotica</i><b>?</b> Please. I've seen more touching in Disney movies.) The psychological harm of the kidnapping I could have gotten over, the mental and physical abuse<b>?</b> SO hard for me. Even though we know she was abused from the opening, the first time he slapped her left me in complete and utter shock. I had to walk away. His behavior was so appalling at times but, being a hopeless romantic, I just kept hoping. I'm still hoping. I convinced myself that it was going to be okay and that maybe I could deal with the physical abuse and breakdown because they were in love. Maybe she could change him -- maybe she could make him a better man. Then the ending happen.. I have to say that I perfected my "<i>WTF</i>" face reading this. I thought that the back story was going to FIX him, not take him to a new level of scary. Every single thing was planned and calculated to perfection. He is a cruel vindictive man so blinded by his immeasurable hate for Claire's grandfather, he couldn't care less that the man is dead and Claire had nothing to do with what went down in his past. Anthony Rawlings is a manipulative SOB. He'll make Abu Nazir proud with his torture tactics and maniacal scheming.<br /><br /><u>What is this mind-fuck everyone is talking about</u><b>?</b> <br /><br />We the reader LIVE the mental abuse with Claire. At first I was very angry with her for not trying harder to escape but eventually Anthony’s abuse got to me as well, until I was shouting at the book "<i>Claire don’t do that you are going to make him so angry, please just make him happy</i>". You actually begin to suffer from fear of knowing that this next step, this next move, could mess with Anthony's (as so many times reminded) appearance. Would Anthony be mad and we would suffer for it or would he be nice and reward us<b>?</b> Countless times I had to remind myself that I should not be worried about pleasing this man but plotting with Optimist on how to rip his balls off with our teeth. He just has no redeemable qualities what so ever. It will honestly take a miracle for me to read TRUTH without tearing the damn thing in half. I have no desire or see any fathomable reasoning as to how these two could ever have an HEA and I don’t want one. What I want more than anything is for Claire to find just one vulnerability in Anthony, one thing he might covet or care for and then I want her to destroy it in front of him and literally bring him to his knees.<br /><br />Now let's back up this '<i>I Want to Murder Anthony</i>' train a bit to the cause of this whole mess. The man she respected and liked just RAPED and abused her. (Obviously.) Then he starts telling her she signed a work contract allowing him carte blanche. - Huh<b>?</b> When he spoke of the arrangement, my first thought was, “<i>Dude, tell him that crap don’t fly morally OR legally</i>.” I mean she even recalls the whole night, after gaining her bearings, and KNOWS that she only signed a crappy little napkin that I would of ripped from the man's pocket and blown my nose on.. Point<b>?</b> Why the hell does she act so surprised when she sees the napkin for the second time<b>?</b> He got us Claie. He got us good. But can we just move on to plotting sweet, sweet revenge<b>?</b> (Whoever said revenge is not the answer clearly never met Anthony.) For every freedom Claire felt she won, she was really being mocked by Anthony. Now THAT would've been the punch to my gut. Hell, I'd rather have that shocking smack to the face then feel like a played puppy. Just thinking that all the pain he put me through was a small victory for him<b>?</b> Oh-helllll-no<b>!</b> Speaking about seeing that napkin again.. I laughed my arse off about his note. I think he seriously overplayed his hand there. “<i>Does he want a ‘well done’</i>?” *<b>shaking my head</b>* <br /><br /><u>Why not rate it a perfect 5</u><b>?</b><br /><br />The first half of the book kept me riveted, but then it spirals out of control in this never ending drama and non-stop introspective from Claire who acts immature and naïve at times. She’s very angry and hurt at first, as well as scared, and does try to fight, but I felt she succumbed too quickly and her falling for Tony felt fake. In a domestic situation you know your perpetrator. They take the time to seduce you (not in the sexual sense). They manipulate, use cunningness, and warp your mind. This creates the perfect victim who somehow blames themselves for every negative word and touch. In this instance, it was abduction. You can’t go between terror and adoration within an hour. The need to please and not disappoint was properly written. It was the emotions that lead up to the all-encompassing need to please their victimizer that was missing. That is where a star was removed.<br /><br />This novel was huge and I agree with others in the fact that it could have been worked down to half. The author goes into a lot of details and scene setups that I believe could have been left out. Do not force scenes to fill a quota on what you believe creates a finished book. I don’t know if this is the reason for the repetitive nature, but I can see that it could be. Althea also makes the mistake of jumping into Tony’s POV as if to try and explain why he acts the way he does. That's a big no-no because it ruins the entire thriller element that’s slowly building, which when all is said and done, never delivers.<br /><br /><u>Will therapy be required after this read</u><b>?</b><br /><br />I believe so. And it is only fair that we ALL place of our therapist bills on Anthony's tab.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4825612510740339413" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/435197017?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12416934-consequences">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=mind-fuckery">mind-fuckery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer435197017" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7567809678496135403">Well....well....well..... <br/><br/>"Hello, Claire." I swear Hannibal Lector came to mind on more than one occasion in this book. <br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=368720976b3f5158fe85c3b6d2b16ad0_zpsef6cbbfd.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381495204i/4943858.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=82f0ffdb5c0084c2415f0b32e7b18323_zpsce030ed0.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381109698i/4232001._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I'd like to say the second time around reading this I enjoyed it just as much. Unfortunately, I dropped my rating to four stars. Still, that's a great book, just not stellar. I found myself bored with all the insane details throughout this book. By around 60% I was skimming.....pages upon pages of skimming. I don't need a play by play of their diet, her wardrobe, what t</span>
  <span id="freeText7567809678496135403" style="display:none">Well....well....well..... <br><br>"Hello, Claire." I swear Hannibal Lector came to mind on more than one occasion in this book. <br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=368720976b3f5158fe85c3b6d2b16ad0_zpsef6cbbfd.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381495204i/4943858.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=82f0ffdb5c0084c2415f0b32e7b18323_zpsce030ed0.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381109698i/4232001._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'd like to say the second time around reading this I enjoyed it just as much. Unfortunately, I dropped my rating to four stars. Still, that's a great book, just not stellar. I found myself bored with all the insane details throughout this book. By around 60% I was skimming.....pages upon pages of skimming. I don't need a play by play of their diet, her wardrobe, what they did every minute of every day on vacation in Europe. Give me the mind fuckery that's everything awesome about this series! <br><br>Reviewing this book is impossible without giving away plot. It's mysterious, captivating and dark. Why it's tagged erotica, I have no clue. This is NOT erotica. <br><br>Tony Rawlings.... I have one word for you...<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_le6n23ijWm1qd5525o1_500_zpsdc8c2230.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381454179ra/4887481.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'd love to say I'm on team Tony but nope...and I've read Truth. Still not on a Team Tony. Felonies are hard for me to swallow. You belong in prison. Two more words for you....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=gif-2_zpsb39c06dc.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381454179ra/4887482.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Or maybe these two words.....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr-officerkalakua_zpsd57e3d38.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381454179ra/4887483.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now Claire, I'll try and forgive you for being a weak, pathetic heroine for this whole book. You survived, I get it. But in the end.....you rock!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=bitches_zpsbf2d8dd0.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381454179ra/4887484.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, this will NOT be a response from reading this book! Expect the opposite!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=fullofrainbows_zpsae5bab58.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381454179ra/4887485.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A little more along the lines of....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=mindfuck_zps88bfafd3.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/621180.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, consider yourself warned. It's a great story, a great ride, but zero hearts and flowers people! I'll be a masochist and continue on.....</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('d5ciZ9ev8YOaPesAEkpxSEOAQl8T5AmdWPqfJNLwWkDk37l38YPRhsJUmF0I8BCX5VQNNTjJJdqW30EtnIArTw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('m7GX7E2Qs1nXfSMd7dVGPydLLb+gQbJ7WLsvSv7d524I+Qz8a7yTXI8UUED3byfggZ9i1YtsnjyWnvFDsK2WYQ==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/5131072.Aleatha_Romig">About Aleatha Romig</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/5131072.Aleatha_Romig"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1445297443p3/5131072.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3740479521308417625">Aleatha Romig is a New York Times, Wall Street Journal, and USA Today bestselling author who lives in Indiana, USA. She grew up in Mishawaka, graduated from Indiana University, and is currently living south of Indianapolis. Aleatha has raised three children with her high school sweetheart and husband of over thirty years. Before she became a full-time author, she worked days as a dental hygienist </span>
  <span id="freeText3740479521308417625" style="display:none">Aleatha Romig is a New York Times, Wall Street Journal, and USA Today bestselling author who lives in Indiana, USA. She grew up in Mishawaka, graduated from Indiana University, and is currently living south of Indianapolis. Aleatha has raised three children with her high school sweetheart and husband of over thirty years. Before she became a full-time author, she worked days as a dental hygienist and spent her nights writing. Now, when she's not imagining mind-blowing twists and turns, she likes to spend her time with her family and friends. Her other pastimes include reading and creating heroes/anti-heroes who haunt your dreams!<br /><br />Aleatha released her first novel, CONSEQUENCES, in August of 2011. CONSEQUENCES became a bestselling series with five novels and two companions released from 2011 through 2015. The compelling and epic story of Anthony and Claire Rawlings has graced more than half a million e-readers. Aleatha released the first of her series TALES FROM THE DARK SIDE, INSIDIOUS, in the fall of 2014. These stand-alone thrillers continue Aleatha's twisted style with an increase in heat. <br /><br />In the fall of 2015, Aleatha moved headfirst into the world of dark romantic suspense saga with the release of BETRAYAL, the first of her five-novel INFIDELITY series that has taken the reading world by storm. She also began her traditional publishing career with Thomas and Mercer. Her books INTO THE LIGHT and AWAY FROM THE DARK were published through this mystery/thriller publisher in 2016.<br /><br />In the spring of 2017, Aleatha released her first stand-alone, fun, and sexy romantic comedy PLUS ONE, followed by ONE NIGHT, and ANOTHER ONE. Her range of genres includes erotic romance novellas in her INDULGENCE series.<br /><br />Aleatha returned to her dark roots in 2018 with WEB OF SIN, a dark romantic trilogy with an all new anti-hero. The Sparrow Webs continued with TANGLED WEB, WEB OF DESIRE, and soon DANGEROUS WEB. <br /><br />Aleatha is a "Published Author's Network" member of the Romance Writers of America, NINC, and PEN America. She is represented by Kevan Lyon of Marsal Lyon Literary Agency. Her marketing is represented by Wildfire Marketing.<br /></span>
